    "舊約-- 創世記(Genesis) -- 第1 章( 本篇共有50 章)    　\n\n\n1:1    起初神創造天地。\nIn the beginning God created the heaven and the earth.\n\n1:2    地是空虛混沌。淵面黑暗。神的靈執行在水面上。\nAnd the earth was without form, and void; and darkness was upon the face of the deep. And the Spirit of God moved upon the face of the waters.\n\n1:3    神說，要有光，就有了光。\nAnd God said, Let there be light: and there was light.\n\n1:4    神看光是好的，就把光暗分開了。\nAnd God saw the light, that it was good: and God divided the light from the darkness.\n\n1:5    神稱光為晝",
    "神稱光為晝，稱暗為夜。有晚上，有早晨，這是頭一日。\nAnd God called the light Day, and the darkness he called Night. And the evening and the morning were the first day.\n\n1:6    神說，諸水之間要有空氣，將水分為上下。\nAnd God said, Let there be a firmament in the midst of the waters, and let it divide the waters from the waters.\n\n1:7    神就造出空氣，將空氣以下的水，空氣以上的水分開了。事就這樣成了。\nAnd God made the firmament, and divided the waters which were under the firmament from the waters which were above the firmament: and it was so.\n\n1:8    神稱空氣為天。有晚",
    "。有晚上，有早晨，是第二日。\nAnd God called the firmament Heaven. And the evening and the morning were the second day.\n\n1:9    神說，天下的水要聚在一處，使旱地露出來。事就這樣成了。\nAnd God said, Let the waters under the heaven be gathered together unto one place, and let the dry land appear: and it was so.\n\n1:10    神稱旱地為地，稱水的聚處為海。神看是好的。\nAnd God called the dry land Earth; and the gathering together of the waters called he Seas: and God saw that it was good.\n\n1:11    神說，地要發生青草，和結種子的菜蔬，並結果子的樹木，各從其類，",
    "神說，地要發生青草，和結種子的菜蔬，並結果子的樹木，各從其類，果子都包著核。事就這樣成了。\nAnd God said, Let the earth bring forth grass, the herb yielding seed, and the fruit tree yielding fruit after his kind, whose seed is in itself, upon the earth: and it was so.\n\n1:12    於是地發生了青草，和結種子的菜蔬，各從其類，並結果子的樹木，各從其類，果子都包著核。神看著是好的。\nAnd the earth brought forth grass, and herb yielding seed after his kind, and the tree yielding fruit, whose seed was in itself, after his kind: and God saw that it was good.\n\n1:13    有晚上，有早晨，是第三日。\nAnd the evening and the morning were the",
    "third day.\n\n1:14    神說，天上要有光體，可以分晝夜，作記號，定節令，日子，年歲。\nAnd God said, Let there be lights in the firmament of the heaven to divide the day from the night; and let them be for signs, and for seasons, and for days, and years:\n\n1:15    並要發光在天空，普照在地上。事就這樣成了。\nAnd let them be for lights in the firmament of the heaven to give light upon the earth: and it was so.\n\n1:16    於是神造了兩個大光，大的管晝，小的管夜。又造眾星。\nAnd God made two great lights; the greater light to rule the day, and the lesser light to rule the n",
    "night: he made the stars also.\n\n1:17    就把這些光擺列在天空，普照在地上。\nAnd God set them in the firmament of the heaven to give light upon the earth,\n\n1:18    管理晝夜，分別明暗。神看著是好的。\nAnd to rule over the day and over the night, and to divide the light from the darkness: and God saw that it was good.\n\n1:19    有晚上，有早晨，是第四日。\nAnd the evening and the morning were the fourth day.\n\n1:20    神說，水要多多滋生有生命的物，要有雀鳥飛在地面以上，天空之中。\nAnd God said, Let the waters bring forth abundantly the moving creature that hath life,",

    "created he him; male and female created he them.\n\n1:28    神就賜福給他們，又對他們說，要生養眾多，遍滿地面，治理這地。也要管理海里的魚，空中的鳥，和地上各樣行動的活物。\nAnd God blessed them, and God said unto them, Be fruitful, and multiply, and replenish the earth, and subdue it: and have dominion over the fish of the sea, and over the fowl of the air, and over every living thing that moveth upon the earth.\n\n1:29    神說，看哪，我將遍地上一切結種子的菜蔬和一切樹上所結有核的果子，全賜給你們作食物。\nAnd God said, Behold, I have given you ev",
    "every herb bearing seed, which is upon the face of all the earth, and every tree, in the which is the fruit of a tree yielding seed; to you it shall be for meat.\n\n1:30    至於地上的走獸和空中的飛鳥，並各樣爬在地上有生命的物，我將青草賜給它們作食物。事就這樣成了。\nAnd to every beast of the earth, and to every fowl of the air, and to every thing that creepeth upon the earth, wherein there is life, I have given every green herb for meat: and it was so.\n\n1:31    神看著一切所造的都甚好。有晚上，有早晨，是第六日。\nAnd God saw every thing that he had made, and, behold, it",
    "it was very good. And the evening and the morning were the sixth day.\n\n\n\n\n舊約-- 創世記(Genesis) -- 第2 章( 本篇共有50 章)    　\n\n\n2:1    天地萬物都造齊了。\nThus the heavens and the earth were finished, and all the host of them.\n\n2:2    到第七日，神造物的工已經完畢，就在第七日歇了他一切的工，安息了。\nAnd on the seventh day God ended his work which he had made; and he rested on the seventh day from all his work which he had made.\n\n2:3    神賜福給第七日，定為聖日，因為在這日神歇了他一切創造的工，就安息了。\nAnd God blessed the seventh day, and sanctif",
    "sanctified it: because that in it he had rested from all his work which God created and made.\n\n2:4    創造天地的來歷，在耶和華神造天地的日子，乃是這樣。\nThese are the generations of the heavens and of the earth when they were created, in the day that the LORD God made the earth and the heavens,\n\n2:5    野地還沒有草木，田間的菜蔬還沒有長起來，因為耶和華神還沒有降雨在地上，也沒有人耕地。\nAnd every plant of the field before it was in the earth, and every herb of the field before it grew: for the LORD God had not caused it to rain upon the earth, and there was not a man to till",
    "till the ground.\n\n2:6    但有霧氣從地上騰，滋潤遍地。\nBut there went up a mist from the earth, and watered the whole face of the ground.\n\n2:7    耶和華神用地上的塵土造人，將生氣吹在他鼻孔裡，他就成了有靈的活人，名叫亞當。\nAnd the LORD God formed man of the dust of the ground, and breathed into his nostrils the breath of life; and man became a living soul.\n\n2:8    耶和華神在東方的伊甸立了一個園子，把所造的人安置在那裡。\nAnd the LORD God planted a garden eastward in Eden; and there he put the man whom he had formed.\n\n2:9    耶和華神使各樣的樹從地裡",

    "which compasseth the whole land of Havilah, where there is gold;\n\n2:12    並且那地的金子是好的。在那裡又有珍珠和紅瑪瑙。\nAnd the gold of that land is good: there is bdellium and the onyx stone.\n\n2:13    第二道河名叫基訓，就是環繞古實全地的。\nAnd the name of the second river is Gihon: the same is it that compasseth the whole land of Ethiopia.\n\n2:14    第三道河名叫西底結，流在亞述的東邊。第四道河就是幼發拉底河。\nAnd the name of the third river is Hiddekel: that is it which goeth toward the east of Assyria. And the fourth river is Euphrates.\n\n2:15    耶和華神",

    "。只是那人沒有遇見配偶幫助他。\nAnd Adam gave names to all cattle, and to the fowl of the air, and to every beast of the field; but for Adam there was not found an help meet for him.\n\n2:21    耶和華神使他沉睡，他就睡了。於是取下他的一條肋骨，又把肉合起來。\nAnd the LORD God caused a deep sleep to fall upon Adam, and he slept: and he took one of his ribs, and closed up the flesh instead thereof;\n\n2:22    耶和華神就用那人身上所取的肋骨，造成一個女人，領她到那人跟前。\nAnd the rib, which the LORD God had taken from man, made he a woman, and brought her unto the man.\n\n2:23    那人說，這是我",

And the woman said, The serpent beguiled me, and I did eat.\n\n3:14    耶和華神對蛇說，你既",

    "耶和華神便打發他出伊甸園去，耕種他所自出之土。\nTherefore the LORD God sent him forth from the garden of Eden, to till the ground from whence he was taken.\n\n3:24    於是把他趕出去了。又在伊甸園的東邊安設基路伯和四面轉動發火焰的劍，要把守生命樹的道路。\nSo he drove out the man; and he placed at the east of the garden of Eden Cherubims, and a flaming sword which turned every way, to keep the way of the tree of life.\n\n\n\n\n舊約-- 創世記(Genesis) -- 第4 章( 本篇共有50 章)    　\n\n\n4:1    有一日，那人和他妻子夏娃同房。夏娃就懷孕，生了該隱（就是得的意思",
    "。夏娃就懷孕，生了該隱（就是得的意思），便說，耶和華使我得了一個男子。\nAnd Adam knew Eve his wife; and she conceived, and bare Cain, and said, I have gotten a man from the LORD.\n\n4:2    又生了該隱的兄弟亞伯。亞伯是牧羊的，該隱是種地的。\nAnd she again bare his brother Abel. And Abel was a keeper of sheep, but Cain was a tiller of the ground.\n\n4:3    有一日，該隱拿地裡的出產為供物獻給耶和華。\nAnd in process of time it came to pass, that Cain brought of the fruit of the ground an offering unto the LORD.\n\n4:4    亞伯也將他羊群中頭生的和羊的脂油獻上。耶和華看中了亞伯和他的供物，\nA",
    "。耶和華看中了亞伯和他的供物，\nAnd Abel, he also brought of the firstlings of his flock and of the fat thereof.     "我們要起來，上伯特利去，在那裡我要築一座壇給神，就是在我遭難的日子應允我的禱告，在我行的路上保佑我的那位。\nAnd let us arise, and go up to Bethel; and I will make there an altar unto God, who answered me in the day of my distress, and was with me in the way which I went.\n\n35:4    他們就把外邦人的神像和他們耳朵上的環子交給雅各。雅各都藏在示劍那裡的橡樹底下。\nAnd they gave unto Jacob all the strange gods which were in their hand, and all their earrings which were in their ears; and Jacob hid them under the oak which was by Shechem.\n\n35:5    他們便起行前往。",
    "。神使那周圍城邑的人都甚驚懼，就不追趕雅各的眾子了。\nAnd they journeyed: and the terror of God was upon the cities that were round about them, and they did not pursue after the sons of Jacob.\n\n35:6    於是雅各和一切與他同在的人到了迦南地的路斯，就是伯特利。\nSo Jacob came to Luz, which is in the land of Canaan, that is, Bethel, he and all the people that were with him.\n\n35:7    他在那裡築了一座壇，就給那地方起名叫伊勒伯特利（就是伯特利之神的意思），因為他逃避他哥哥的時候，神在那裡向他顯現。\nAnd he built there an altar, and called",

    "Isaac gave up the ghost, and died, and was gathered unto his people, being old and full of days: and his sons Esau and Jacob buried him.\n\n\n\n\n舊約-- 創世記(Genesis) -- 第36 章( 本篇共有50 章)    　\n\n\n36:1    以掃就是以東，他的後代記在下面。\nNow these are the generations of Esau, who is Edom.\n\n36:2    以掃娶迦南的女子為妻，就是赫人以倫的女兒亞大和希未人祭便的孫女，亞拿的女兒阿何利巴瑪，\nEsau took his wives of the daughters of Canaan; Adah the daughter of Elon the Hittite, and Aholibamah the daughter of Anah the daughter of Zibeon the Hivite;\n\n36:3    又娶了以",
    "又娶了以實瑪利的女兒，尼拜約的妹子巴實抹。\nAnd Bashemath Ishmael's daughter, sister of Nebajoth.\n\n36:4    亞大給以掃生了以利法。巴實抹生了流珥。\nAnd Adah bare to Esau Eliphaz; and Bashemath bare Reuel;\n\n36:5    阿何利巴瑪生了耶烏施，雅蘭，可拉。這都是以掃的兒子，是在迦南地生的。\nAnd Aholibamah bare Jeush, and Jaalam, and Korah: these are the sons of Esau, which were born unto him in the land of Canaan.\n\n36:6    以掃帶著他的妻子，兒女，與家中一切的人口，並他的牛羊，牲畜，和一切貨財，就是他在迦南地所得的，往別處去，離了他",
    "兄弟雅各。\nAnd Esau took his wives, and his sons, and his daughters, and all the persons of his house, and his cattle, and all his beasts, and all his substance, which he had got in the land of Canaan; and went into the country from the face of his brother Jacob.\n\n36:7    因為二人的財物群畜甚多，寄居的地方容不下他們，所以不能同居。\nFor their riches were more than that they might dwell together; and the land wherein they were strangers could not bear them because of their cattle.\n\n36:8    於是以掃住在西珥山裡。以掃就是以東。\nThus dwelt Esau in mount Seir: Esau is Edom.\n\n36:9    以",

    "him, and kissed him.\n\n50:2    約瑟吩咐伺候他的醫生用香料薰他父親，醫生就用香料薰了以色列。\nAnd Joseph commanded his servants the physicians to embalm his father: and the physicians embalmed Israel.\n\n50:3    薰屍的常例是四十天。那四十天滿了，埃及人為他哀哭了七十天。\nAnd forty days were fulfilled for him; for so are fulfilled the days of those which are embalmed: and the Egyptians mourned for him threescore and ten days.\n\n50:4    為他哀哭的日子過了，約瑟對法老家中的人說，我若在你們眼前蒙恩，請你們報告法老說，\nAnd when the days of his mourn",
    "mourning were past, Joseph spake unto the house of Pharaoh, saying, If now I have found grace in your eyes, speak, I pray you, in the ears of Pharaoh, saying,\n\n50:5    我父親要死的時候叫我起誓說，你要將我葬在迦南地，在我為自己所掘的墳墓裡。現在求你讓我上去葬我父親，以後我必回來。\nMy father made me swear, saying, Lo, I die: in my grave which I have digged for me in the land of Canaan, there shalt thou bury me. Now therefore let me go up, I pray thee, and bury my father, and I will come again.\n\n50:6    法老說，你可以上去，照著你父親叫你起的誓，將他葬埋。\nAnd",
    "Pharaoh said, Go up, and bury thy father, according as he made thee swear.\n\n50:7    於是約瑟上去葬他父親。與他一同上去的，有法老的臣僕和法老家中的長老，並埃及國的長老，\nAnd Joseph went up to bury his father: and with him went up all the servants of Pharaoh, the elders of his house, and all the elders of the land of Egypt,\n\n50:8    還有約瑟的全家和他的弟兄們，並他父親的眷屬。只有他們的婦人孩子，和羊群牛群，都留在歌珊地。\nAnd all the house of Joseph, and his brethren, and his father's house: only their little ones, and their flocks, and their herds,",
    "herds, they left in the land of Goshen.\n\n50:9    又有車輛馬兵，和他一同上去。那一幫人甚多。\nAnd there went up with him both chariots and horsemen: and it was a very great company.\n\n50:10    他們到了約旦河外，亞達的禾場，就在那裡大大地號啕痛哭。約瑟為他父親哀哭了七天。\nAnd they came to the threshingfloor of Atad, which is beyond Jordan, and there they mourned with a great and very sore lamentation: and he made a mourning for his father seven days.\n\n50:11    迦南的居民見亞達禾場上的哀哭，就說，這是埃及人一場大的哀哭。因此那地方名叫亞伯麥西",
    "。因此那地方名叫亞伯麥西，是在約旦河東。\nAnd when the inhabitants of the land, the Canaanites, saw the mourning in the floor of Atad, they said, This is a grievous mourning to the Egyptians: wherefore the name of it was called Abelmizraim, which is beyond Jordan.\n\n50:12    雅各的兒子們就遵著他父親所吩咐的辦了，\nAnd his sons did unto him according as he commanded them:\n\n50:13    把他搬到迦南地，葬在幔利前，麥比拉田間的洞裡。那洞和田是亞伯拉罕向赫人以弗侖買來為業，作墳地的。\nFor his sons carried him into the land of Canaan, and buried him in the cave of the field of Machpelah, which Abr",
    "Abraham bought with the field for a possession of a buryingplace of Ephron the Hittite, before Mamre.\n\n50:14    約瑟葬了他父親以後，就和眾弟兄，並一切同他上去葬他父親的人，都回埃及去了。\nAnd Joseph returned into Egypt, he, and his brethren, and all that went up with him to bury his father, after he had buried his father.\n\n50:15    約瑟的哥哥們見父親死了，就說，或者約瑟懷恨我們，照著我們從前待他一切的惡足足地報復我們。\nAnd when Joseph's brethren saw that their father was dead, they said, Joseph will peradventure hate us, and will certainly requite us all th",
    "the evil which we did unto him.\n\n50:16    他們就打發人去見約瑟，說，你父親未死以先吩咐說，\nAnd they sent a messenger unto Joseph, saying, Thy father did command before he died, saying,\n\n50:17    你們要對約瑟這樣說，從前你哥哥們惡待你，求你饒恕他們的過犯和罪惡。如今求你饒恕你父親神之僕人的過犯。他們對約瑟說這話，約瑟就哭了。\nSo shall ye say unto Joseph, Forgive, I pray thee now, the trespass of thy brethren, and their sin; for they did unto thee evil: and now, we pray thee, forgive the trespass of the servants of the God of thy father.     "wept when they spake unto him.\n\n50:18    他的哥哥們又來俯伏在他面前，說，我們是你的僕人。\nAnd his brethren also went and fell down before his face; and they said, Behold, we be thy servants.\n\n50:19    約瑟對他們說，不要害怕，我豈能代替神呢。\nAnd Joseph said unto them, Fear not: for am I in the place of God?\n\n50:20    從前你們的意思是要害我，但神的意思原是好的，要保全許多人的性命，成就今日的光景。\nBut as for you, ye thought evil against me; but God meant it unto good, to bring to pass, as it is this day, to save much people alive.\n\n50:21    現在你",
